 2640 happyNewToken action sts stk [] =
 2641         happyDoAction 51# notHappyAtAll action sts stk []
 2642 
 2643 happyNewToken action sts stk (tk:tks) =
 2644         let cont i = happyDoAction i tk action sts stk tks in
 2645         case tk of {
 2646         TReserved _ "import" -> cont 1#;
 2647         TReserved _ "submodule" -> cont 2#;
 2648         TReserved _ "and" -> cont 3#;
 2649         TReserved _ "as" -> cont 4#;
 2650         TReserved _ "hiding" -> cont 5#;
 2651         TReserved _ "let" -> cont 6#;
 2652         TReserved _ "rec" -> cont 7#;
 2653         TReserved _ "in" -> cont 8#;
 2654         TReserved _ "do" -> cont 9#;
 2655         TReserved _ "if" -> cont 10#;
 2656         TReserved _ "then" -> cont 11#;
 2657         TReserved _ "else" -> cont 12#;
 2658         TReserved _ "typedef" -> cont 13#;
 2659         TReserved _ "rebindable" -> cont 14#;
 2660         TReserved _ "ProofScript" -> cont 15#;
 2661         TReserved _ "TopLevel" -> cont 16#;
 2662         TReserved _ "CrucibleSetup" -> cont 17#;
 2663         TReserved _ "CrucibleMethodSpec" -> cont 18#;
 2664         TReserved _ "LLVMSpec" -> cont 19#;
 2665         TReserved _ "JVMMethodSpec" -> cont 20#;
 2666         TReserved _ "JVMSpec" -> cont 21#;
 2667         TReserved _ "MIRSpec" -> cont 22#;
 2668         TReserved _ "Bool" -> cont 23#;
 2669         TReserved _ "Int" -> cont 24#;
 2670         TReserved _ "String" -> cont 25#;
 2671         TReserved _ "Term" -> cont 26#;
 2672         TReserved _ "Type" -> cont 27#;
 2673         TReserved _ "AIG" -> cont 28#;
 2674         TReserved _ "CFG" -> cont 29#;
 2675         TPunct    _ ";" -> cont 30#;
 2676         TPunct    _ "[" -> cont 31#;
 2677         TPunct    _ "]" -> cont 32#;
 2678         TPunct    _ "(" -> cont 33#;
 2679         TPunct    _ ")" -> cont 34#;
 2680         TPunct    _ "{" -> cont 35#;
 2681         TPunct    _ "}" -> cont 36#;
 2682         TPunct    _ ":" -> cont 37#;
 2683         TPunct    _ "::" -> cont 38#;
 2684         TPunct    _ "," -> cont 39#;
 2685         TPunct    _ "." -> cont 40#;
 2686         TPunct    _ "\\" -> cont 41#;
 2687         TPunct    _ "=" -> cont 42#;
 2688         TPunct    _ "->" -> cont 43#;
 2689         TPunct    _ "<-" -> cont 44#;
 2690         TLit      _ _ -> cont 45#;
 2691         TCode     _ _ -> cont 46#;
 2692         TCType    _ _ -> cont 47#;
 2693         TNum      _ _ _ -> cont 48#;
 2694         TVar      _ _ -> cont 49#;
 2695         TEOF      _ _ -> cont 50#;
 2696         _ -> happyError' ((tk:tks), [])
 2697         }
 2698 
 2699 happyError_ explist 51# tk tks = happyError' (tks, explist)
 2700 happyError_ explist _ tk tks = happyError' ((tk:tks), explist)
 2701 
 2702 happyThen :: () => Either ParseError a -> (a -> Either ParseError b) -> Either ParseError b
 2703 happyThen = (Prelude.>>=)
 2704 happyReturn :: () => a -> Either ParseError a
 2705 happyReturn = (Prelude.return)
 2706 happyThen1 m k tks = (Prelude.>>=) m (\a -> k a tks)
 2707 happyReturn1 :: () => a -> b -> Either ParseError a
 2708 happyReturn1 = \a tks -> (Prelude.return) a
 2709 happyError' :: () => ([(Token Pos)], [Prelude.String]) -> Either ParseError a
 2710 happyError' = (\(tokens, _) -> parseError tokens)
 2711 parseModule tks = happySomeParser where
 2712  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 0# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap9 x') = happyOut9 x} in x'))
 2713 
 2714 parseStmt tks = happySomeParser where
 2715  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 1# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap10 x') = happyOut10 x} in x'))
 2716 
 2717 parseStmtSemi tks = happySomeParser where
 2718  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 2# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap11 x') = happyOut11 x} in x'))
 2719 
 2720 parseExpression tks = happySomeParser where
 2721  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 3# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap12 x') = happyOut12 x} in x'))
 2722 
 2723 parseSchema tks = happySomeParser where
 2724  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 4# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap13 x') = happyOut13 x} in x'))
 2725 
 2726 parseSchemaPattern tks = happySomeParser where
 2727  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 5# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap14 x') = happyOut14 x} in x'))
 2728 
 2729 happySeq = happyDontSeq

 2732 data ParseError
 2733   = UnexpectedEOF
 2734   | UnexpectedToken (Token Pos)
 2735   | InvalidPattern Expr
 2736   | EmptyBlock Pos
 2737   | InvalidBlock Pos
 2738 
 2739 instance Exception ParseError
 2740 
 2741 instance Show ParseError where
 2742   show e =
 2743     case e of
 2744       UnexpectedEOF     -> "Parse error: unexpected end of file"
 2745       UnexpectedToken t -> "Parse error at " ++ show (tokPos t) ++ ": Unexpected `" ++ unpack (tokStr t) ++ "'"
 2746         where Range _ sl sc el ec = tokPos t -- TODO show token span consistently
 2747       InvalidPattern x  -> "Parse error: invalid pattern " ++ pShow x
 2748       EmptyBlock pos -> show pos ++ ": do block must include at least one expression"
 2749       InvalidBlock pos -> show pos ++ ": do block must end with expression"
 2750 
 2751 parseError :: [Token Pos] -> Either ParseError b
 2752 parseError toks = case toks of
 2753   []    -> Left UnexpectedEOF
 2754   t : _ -> Left (UnexpectedToken t)
 2755 
 2756 -- | Cons up an import.
 2757 buildImport ::
 2758     Bool ->
 2759     (Either FilePath P.ModName, Pos) ->
 2760     (Maybe P.ModName, Pos) ->
 2761     (Maybe P.ImportSpec, Pos) ->
 2762     Import
 2763 buildImport issub (modName, namePos) (mbAsName, asPos) (mbSpec, specPos) =
 2764   Import {
 2765     iIsSubmodule = issub,
 2766     iModule = modName,
 2767     iAs = mbAsName,
 2768     iSpec = mbSpec,
 2769     iPos = maxSpan [namePos, asPos, specPos]
 2770   }
 2771 
 2772 -- | As seen by the parser, a "function name" is an arbitrary pattern.
 2773 --   This is because we use the same syntax for function and value bindings:
 2774 --   in "let (a, b) = e" the "(a, b)" can and should be an arbitrary pattern.
 2775 --   For functions it doesn't make sense for it to be anything but a plain
 2776 --   name, as in "let f () = e". You can write "let (a, b) () = e" and the
 2777 --   parser will accept it, but it won't typecheck.
 2778 --
 2779 --   This function extracts the actual name, if any, for annotating
 2780 --   the lambda expressions we turn further arguments into. It will
 2781 --   return Nothing if the name is something other than an actual
 2782 --   name, which is fine for value bindings since the result won't be
 2783 --   used and also fine for nonsense like "let (a, b) () = e" that'll
 2784 --   be rejected by the typechecker. The annotations in question are
 2785 --   used only at eval time.
 2786 --
 2787 --   Runs in the Maybe monad for convenience.
 2788 fixFunctionName :: Maybe Pattern -> Maybe Text
 2789 fixFunctionName mname = do
 2790   name <- mname
 2791   case name of
 2792       PWild {} -> Nothing
 2793       PVar _allpos _namepos name _ty -> Just name
 2794       PTuple {} -> Nothing
 2795 
 2796 buildFunction :: Maybe Pattern -> [Pattern] -> Expr -> Expr
 2797 buildFunction mname args e =
 2798   let mname' = fixFunctionName mname
 2799       once :: Pattern -> Expr -> Expr
 2800       once pat e = Lambda (maxSpan' pat e) mname' pat e
 2801   in
 2802   foldr once e args
 2803 
 2804 buildApplication :: [Expr] -> Expr
 2805 buildApplication es =
 2806   foldl1 (\e body -> Application (maxSpan' e body) e body) es
 2807 
 2808 -- | Build a let-statement.
 2809 buildLet :: Pos -> Decl -> Stmt
 2810 buildLet pos d =
 2811   StmtLet pos ReadOnlyVar (NonRecursive d)
 2812 
 2813 -- | Build a rebindable let-statement.
 2814 buildLetRB :: Pos -> Decl -> Stmt
 2815 buildLetRB pos d =
 2816   StmtLet pos RebindableVar (NonRecursive d)
 2817 
 2818 -- | Build a rec-statement.
 2819 buildRec :: Pos -> [Decl] -> Stmt
 2820 buildRec pos ds =
 2821   StmtLet pos ReadOnlyVar (Recursive ds)
 2822 
 2823 -- | Build a variable-pattern. Discard the variable if it's _.
 2824 --
 2825 --   Note: it is probably more appropriate to discard all variables
 2826 --   that _begin_ with an underscore; however, the traditional usage
 2827 --   in ML, Haskell, and also Rust is to treat variables beginning
 2828 --   with underscore as placeholder variables that can still be used
 2829 --   behind your back. That's wrong; however, SAWScript is not the
 2830 --   place to fight this battle...
 2831 --
 2832 buildPVar :: Pos -> Pos -> Text -> Maybe Type -> Pattern
 2833 buildPVar allpos xpos x mty =
 2834   case x of
 2835     "_" -> PWild allpos mty
 2836     _ -> PVar allpos xpos x mty
 2837 
 2838 -- | Pop off the last statement in a do-block, which is required to
 2839 --   be a plain expression, and unpack it to an expression.
 2840 buildBlock :: Pos -> [Stmt] -> Either ParseError Expr
 2841 buildBlock pos stmts = case reverse stmts of
 2842   StmtBind _spos (PWild _patpos _noty) e : revstmts' ->
 2843     Right $ Block pos (reverse revstmts', e)
 2844   [] ->
 2845     Left $ EmptyBlock pos
 2846   _ ->
 2847     Left $ InvalidBlock pos
 2848 
 2849 toPattern :: Expr -> Either ParseError Pattern
 2850 toPattern expr =
 2851   case expr of
 2852     Tuple pos es ->
 2853         PTuple pos `fmap` mapM toPattern es
 2854     TSig pos (Var xpos x) t ->
 2855         return (buildPVar pos xpos x (Just t))
 2856     Var pos x ->
 2857         return (buildPVar pos pos x Nothing)
 2858     _ ->
 2859         Left (InvalidPattern expr)

 2875 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
 2876 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
 2877 #define LT(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.<# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2878 #define GTE(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.>=# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2879 #define EQ(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.==# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2880 #else
 2881 #define LT(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.<# m)
 2882 #define GTE(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.>=# m)
 2883 #define EQ(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.==# m)
 2884 #endif

 2945 infixr 9 `HappyStk`
 2946 data HappyStk a = HappyStk a (HappyStk a)
 2947 
 2948 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2949 -- starting the parse
 2950 
 2951 happyParse start_state = happyNewToken start_state notHappyAtAll notHappyAtAll
 2952 
 2953 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2954 -- Accepting the parse
 2955 
 2956 -- If the current token is ERROR_TOK, it means we've just accepted a partial
 2957 -- parse (a %partial parser).  We must ignore the saved token on the top of
 2958 -- the stack in this case.
 2959 happyAccept 0# tk st sts (_ `HappyStk` ans `HappyStk` _) =
 2960         happyReturn1 ans
 2961 happyAccept j tk st sts (HappyStk ans _) = 
 2962         (happyTcHack j (happyTcHack st)) (happyReturn1 ans)
 2963 
 2964 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2965 -- Arrays only: do the next action
 2966 
 2967 
 2968 
 2969 happyDoAction i tk st
 2970         = {- nothing -}
 2971           case action of
 2972                 0#           -> {- nothing -}
 2973                                      happyFail (happyExpListPerState ((Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (st)) :: Prelude.Int)) i tk st
 2974                 -1#          -> {- nothing -}
 2975                                      happyAccept i tk st
 2976                 n | LT(n,(0# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) -> {- nothing -}
 2977                                                    (happyReduceArr Happy_Data_Array.! rule) i tk st
 2978                                                    where rule = (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# ((Happy_GHC_Exts.negateInt# ((n Happy_GHC_Exts.+# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))))))
 2979                 n                 -> {- nothing -}
 2980                                      happyShift new_state i tk st
 2981                                      where new_state = (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))
 2982    where off    = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyActOffsets st)
 2983          off_i  = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# i)
 2984          check  = if GTE(off_i,(0# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))
 2985                   then EQ(indexShortOffAddr happyCheck off_i, i)
 2986                   else Prelude.False
 2987          action
 2988           | check     = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 2989           | Prelude.otherwise = indexShortOffAddr happyDefActions st
 2990 
 2991 
 2992 
 2993 
 2994 indexShortOffAddr (HappyA# arr) off =
 2995         Happy_GHC_Exts.narrow16Int# i
 2996   where
 2997         i = Happy_GHC_Exts.word2Int# (Happy_GHC_Exts.or# (Happy_GHC_Exts.uncheckedShiftL# high 8#) low)
 2998         high = Happy_GHC_Exts.int2Word# (Happy_GHC_Exts.ord# (Happy_GHC_Exts.indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' Happy_GHC_Exts.+# 1#)))
 2999         low  = Happy_GHC_Exts.int2Word# (Happy_GHC_Exts.ord# (Happy_GHC_Exts.indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 3000         off' = off Happy_GHC_Exts.*# 2#
 3001 
 3002 
 3003 
 3004 
 3005 {-# INLINE happyLt #-}
 3006 happyLt x y = LT(x,y)                                                             
 3007 
 3008 
 3009 readArrayBit arr bit =
 3010     Bits.testBit (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (indexShortOffAddr arr ((unbox_int bit) `Happy_GHC_Exts.iShiftRA#` 4#))) (bit `Prelude.mod` 16)
 3011   where unbox_int (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# x) = x
 3012

 3037 -- Shifting a token
 3038 
 3039 happyShift new_state 0# tk st sts stk@(x `HappyStk` _) =
 3040      let i = (case Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# x of { (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i)) -> i }) in
 3041 --     trace "shifting the error token" $
 3042      happyDoAction i tk new_state (HappyCons (st) (sts)) (stk)
 3043 
 3044 happyShift new_state i tk st sts stk =
 3045      happyNewToken new_state (HappyCons (st) (sts)) ((happyInTok (tk))`HappyStk`stk)
 3046 
 3047 -- happyReduce is specialised for the common cases.
 3048 
 3049 happySpecReduce_0 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3050      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3051 happySpecReduce_0 nt fn j tk st@((action)) sts stk
 3052      = happyGoto nt j tk st (HappyCons (st) (sts)) (fn `HappyStk` stk)
 3053 
 3054 happySpecReduce_1 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3055      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3056 happySpecReduce_1 nt fn j tk _ sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))) (v1`HappyStk`stk')
 3057      = let r = fn v1 in
 3058        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 3059 
 3060 happySpecReduce_2 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3061      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3062 happySpecReduce_2 nt fn j tk _ (HappyCons (_) (sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))))) (v1`HappyStk`v2`HappyStk`stk')
 3063      = let r = fn v1 v2 in
 3064        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 3065 
 3066 happySpecReduce_3 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3067      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3068 happySpecReduce_3 nt fn j tk _ (HappyCons (_) ((HappyCons (_) (sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))))))) (v1`HappyStk`v2`HappyStk`v3`HappyStk`stk')
 3069      = let r = fn v1 v2 v3 in
 3070        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 3071 
 3072 happyReduce k i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3073      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3074 happyReduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk
 3075      = case happyDrop (k Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) sts of
 3076          sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 3077                 let r = fn stk in  -- it doesn't hurt to always seq here...
 3078                 happyDoSeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st1 sts1 r)
 3079 
 3080 happyMonadReduce k nt fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3081      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3082 happyMonadReduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk =
 3083       case happyDrop k (HappyCons (st) (sts)) of
 3084         sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 3085           let drop_stk = happyDropStk k stk in
 3086           happyThen1 (fn stk tk) (\r -> happyGoto nt j tk st1 sts1 (r `HappyStk` drop_stk))
 3087 
 3088 happyMonad2Reduce k nt fn 0# tk st sts stk
 3089      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 3090 happyMonad2Reduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk =
 3091       case happyDrop k (HappyCons (st) (sts)) of
 3092         sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 3093          let drop_stk = happyDropStk k stk
 3094 
 3095              off = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyGotoOffsets st1)
 3096              off_i = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# nt)
 3097              new_state = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 3098 
 3099 
 3100 
 3101 
 3102           in
 3103           happyThen1 (fn stk tk) (\r -> happyNewToken new_state sts1 (r `HappyStk` drop_stk))
 3104 
 3105 happyDrop 0# l = l
 3106 happyDrop n (HappyCons (_) (t)) = happyDrop (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) t
 3107 
 3108 happyDropStk 0# l = l
 3109 happyDropStk n (x `HappyStk` xs) = happyDropStk (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1#::Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) xs
 3110 
 3111 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3112 -- Moving to a new state after a reduction
 3113 
 3114 
 3115 happyGoto nt j tk st = 
 3116    {- nothing -}
 3117    happyDoAction j tk new_state
 3118    where off = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyGotoOffsets st)
 3119          off_i = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# nt)
 3120          new_state = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 3121 
 3122 
 3123 
 3124 
 3125 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3126 -- Error recovery (ERROR_TOK is the error token)
 3127 
 3128 -- parse error if we are in recovery and we fail again
 3129 happyFail explist 0# tk old_st _ stk@(x `HappyStk` _) =
 3130      let i = (case Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# x of { (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i)) -> i }) in
 3131 --      trace "failing" $ 
 3132         happyError_ explist i tk
 3133 
 3134 {-  We don't need state discarding for our restricted implementation of
 3135     "error".  In fact, it can cause some bogus parses, so I've disabled it
 3136     for now --SDM
 3137 
 3138 -- discard a state
 3139 happyFail  ERROR_TOK tk old_st CONS(HAPPYSTATE(action),sts) 
 3140                                                 (saved_tok `HappyStk` _ `HappyStk` stk) =
 3141 --      trace ("discarding state, depth " ++ show (length stk))  $
 3142         DO_ACTION(action,ERROR_TOK,tk,sts,(saved_tok`HappyStk`stk))
 3143 -}
 3144 
 3145 -- Enter error recovery: generate an error token,
 3146 --                       save the old token and carry on.
 3147 happyFail explist i tk (action) sts stk =
 3148 --      trace "entering error recovery" $
 3149         happyDoAction 0# tk action sts ((Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i))) `HappyStk` stk)
 3150 
 3151 -- Internal happy errors:
 3152 
 3153 notHappyAtAll :: a
 3154 notHappyAtAll = Prelude.error "Internal Happy error\n"

 3156 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3157 -- Hack to get the typechecker to accept our action functions
 3158 
 3159 
 3160 happyTcHack :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int# -> a -> a
 3161 happyTcHack x y = y
 3162 {-# INLINE happyTcHack #-}

 3164 
 3165 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3166 -- Seq-ing.  If the --strict flag is given, then Happy emits 
 3167 --      happySeq = happyDoSeq
 3168 -- otherwise it emits
 3169 --      happySeq = happyDontSeq
 3170 
 3171 happyDoSeq, happyDontSeq :: a -> b -> b
 3172 happyDoSeq   a b = a `Prelude.seq` b
 3173 happyDontSeq a b = b
 3174 
 3175 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3176 -- Don't inline any functions from the template.  GHC has a nasty habit
 3177 -- of deciding to inline happyGoto everywhere, which increases the size of
 3178 -- the generated parser quite a bit.
 3179 
 3180 
 3181 {-# NOINLINE happyDoAction #-}
 3182 {-# NOINLINE happyTable #-}
 3183 {-# NOINLINE happyCheck #-}
 3184 {-# NOINLINE happyActOffsets #-}
 3185 {-# NOINLINE happyGotoOffsets #-}
 3186 {-# NOINLINE happyDefActions #-}
 3187 
 3188 {-# NOINLINE happyShift #-}
 3189 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_0 #-}
 3190 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_1 #-}
 3191 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_2 #-}
 3192 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_3 #-}
 3193 {-# NOINLINE happyReduce #-}
 3194 {-# NOINLINE happyMonadReduce #-}
 3195 {-# NOINLINE happyGoto #-}
 3196 {-# NOINLINE happyFail #-}
